A value of 0 means no limit.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies: cnpResource,\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tnsCount:               make(map[string]int),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller loop. A limit of 0\n// means unlimited.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif c.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.nsCount[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"namespace %q has reached the CiliumNetworkPolicy quota of %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// NamespaceCount returns the current number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n// tracked for the given namespace.
